  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_3454a3c5-cc65-4e86-95da-f8ffc96b187b'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();
    }

        if (this.up('#box')) {

<span id="freeTextContainer7822171510325941524"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420429845ra/13223235.gif' width='500' height='245' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>I said I wouldn't let Cassandra screw me over again, yet here I am.</i><br/><br/>So, let me tell you I was absolutely happy when Cassie announced these short stories were coming out because we were going to see how Simon may become a Shadowhunter <b>if he survives the Ascend.</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388923906ra/7957170.gif' width='245' height='270' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Anyhow, here we see how Simon struggles with not remembering everything that happened and we also see how difficult is for everyone else. They, who love him so much and expect him to remember a little more everyday, but that doesn't happen and Simon is afraid, disappointed on himself and lost, so he goes to the Shadowhunter Academy so he can, maybe, be that hero again. Soon, though, he will realize that things aren't the way he expects them to be and he will have to let go in order to move on.<br><br>Cassie,<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424458710ra/13764326.gif" width="500" height="208" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I missed these characters so much but damn, watching them struggling was really hard for me. I cannot really tell you how hard it was. It's like they can't really catch a break. Man.<br>Anyways, I liked how the Academy was set, like we all know how Nephilim are so that wasn't a big surprise but what I absolutely adored was George Lovelace. AWESOME.<br>And you know how I feel about her, right? Like it's her.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424458710ra/13764328.gif" width="300" height="196" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And then we got the end. Bad Cassandra, bad.<br>This story was such an emotional one because we relived some of the losses we got in CoHF and it was all raw new.<br>I need to read the rest of this.</span>

    <a title="Booknut" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6917862-booknut"><img alt="Booknut" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1411194489p2/6917862.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1086296459?book_show_action=true">Oct 21, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Booknut" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Booknut" href="/user/show/6917862-booknut">Booknut</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6917862-booknut?shelf=people-with-powers">people-with-powers</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1086296459" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer766341902577028049"><b>Okay...so the book focuses on Simon.</b><br/><a href='http://photobucket.com/images/meh' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426646180ra/14073555.gif' alt='meh photo: meh joker mehjoker.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/>Simon being the main character was probably one of the few highlights for me in what was otherwise a very 'meh' book. <br/><br/>For those of you who aren't familiar with the term, let me explain:<br/>- Meh refers to ice-cream that isn't blow-your-mind yummy but isn't disgusting either<br/>- It can be used to talk about that one relative of yours you only see at the annual family BBQ<br/>- It's the word Harry Potter fans use to describe characters like Ernie Macmillan or Hannah Abb</span>
  <span id="freeText766341902577028049" style="display:none"><b>Okay...so the book focuses on Simon.</b><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/meh" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426646180ra/14073555.gif" alt="meh photo: meh joker mehjoker.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Simon being the main character was probably one of the few highlights for me in what was otherwise a very 'meh' book. <br><br>For those of you who aren't familiar with the term, let me explain:<br>- Meh refers to ice-cream that isn't blow-your-mind yummy but isn't disgusting either<br>- It can be used to talk about that one relative of yours you only see at the annual family BBQ<br>- It's the word Harry Potter fans use to describe characters like Ernie Macmillan or Hannah Abbott...or Hufflepuff in general (no offense at all to any Hufflepuff lovers! It's a great house.)<br><br>To sum up: if something is 'meh' it just <i>is</i>. It doesn't make you ecstatic, it doesn't wow you, and it also doesn't make you upset/annoyed. It conveys complete indifference.<br><br>I love Cassie Clare's writing. But I feel like the Shadowhunter concept has been dragged out as far as it can go. It feels sort of...boring, you know, reading a book full of characters I've already read about in <i>six books</i> (not counting the other novellas/spin-offs). <br><br>Do I need to rehash Isabelle and Simon's relationship?<br><b>Nope. Been there, done that, got the t-shirt.</b><br>Do I need to be told again how much of an adorable dork Simon is?<br><b>Nope. Been there, done that, got the $5 souvenir.</b><br>Do I need to be reminded that Simon and Clary are great as friends?<br><b>Nope. Been there, done that, saw him get rejected, got a box of tissues.</b><br>Do I need even more explanations of how the Shadowhunter world is run?<br><b>No. Just...no.</b><br><br>Seeing that this series is centered on a Simon who has completely lost is memory (six books worth, I might add) we, the reader, are forced to take a trip back down memory lane. Nearly every chapter is full of déjà vu moments that are a little tiring at times.<br><br><b>It just doesn't feel like a unique book about Simon. It kind of feels like Cassie re-wrote <i>City of Bones</i>, except the main character has memory issues, is male, and is not a redhead.</b><br><br>Hopefully the next few books in this spin-off take the plot to higher levels and really bring home a new tale that truly showcases the Simon we know and love :)<br><br><u>Pre-reading review</u>:<br><b>Simon's getting his own book, guys!</b><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/so%20happy" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413955159ra/11586133.gif" alt="so happy photo: BABY SO HAPPY tumblr_lnfasnQnxY1qavkujo1_500.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/so%20happy" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380385156ra/743977.gif" alt="so happy photo: Happy Endings - Alex Crying tumblr_m4pfv2Uj1J1r3zat8.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/so%20happy" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413955159ra/11586134.gif" alt="so happy photo: tumblr_mmm6wccW2Q1ry1utqo5_250_zps9498333f.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>After everything the poor guy's been through in <i>The Mortal Instruments</i> series, he deserves to have a whole <i>library</i> dedicated to him. It's about time he got his chance in the spotlight!</span>
  <a data-text-id="766341902577028049" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer14790076146302044447"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He had to escape. He had to go and become a hero, the way he had been once.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><b>Oh my sweet, dorky Simon.</b><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22428828.Welcome_to_Shadowhunter_Academy__Tales_from_the_Shadowhunter_Academy___1_' title='Welcome to Shadowhunter Academy (Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy, #1) by Cassandra Clare' rel='nofollow noopener'>Welcome to Shadowhunter Academy</a> brought back all the bitterness and hurt <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8755785.City_of_Heavenly_Fire__The_Mortal_Instruments___6_' title='City of Heavenly Fire (The Mortal Instruments, #6) by Cassandra Clare' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Heavenly Fire</a> provoked, but it wasn't (that much) sad and frustrating. It's true that I am all too eager to find out the person Simon became after the events that took place in Edom, but by the Angel what I really wanted was the trademark Simon sassiness and his witty retorts! This novel offered <b>lots of </b></span>
  <span id="freeText14790076146302044447" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He had to escape. He had to go and become a hero, the way he had been once.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>Oh my sweet, dorky Simon.</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22428828.Welcome_to_Shadowhunter_Academy__Tales_from_the_Shadowhunter_Academy___1_" title="Welcome to Shadowhunter Academy (Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy, #1) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Welcome to Shadowhunter Academy</a> brought back all the bitterness and hurt <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8755785.City_of_Heavenly_Fire__The_Mortal_Instruments___6_" title="City of Heavenly Fire (The Mortal Instruments, #6) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Heavenly Fire</a> provoked, but it wasn't (that much) sad and frustrating. It's true that I am all too eager to find out the person Simon became after the events that took place in Edom, but by the Angel what I really wanted was the trademark Simon sassiness and his witty retorts! This novel offered <b>lots of fun, plenty of laughter</b> and filled me with a sweet longing for all those great moments I experienced while reading The Mortal Instruments! But bringing Jordan into this? That was <b>cruel</b>, Cassie. Cruel, cruel, cruel.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1499109900ra/23192457.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>P.S. Oh, how I've missed you, Lord Montgomery!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5228907476724692273"><b> <i> 4.75/5 stars </i> </b><br/><i> Welcome to Shadowhunter Academy </i> was the first novella in Cassandra Clare's new bind up. I really enjoyed the take on the shadowhunter world from Simon's point of view. I can tell the new, and old, cast of characters are going to mold together perfectly. They all have such unique personalities that play off of each others really well. There were a couple of awkwardly worded scenes and dialogue that didn't flow, but other than that it was beautiful. I recommend starting this coll</span>
  <span id="freeText5228907476724692273" style="display:none"><b> <i> 4.75/5 stars </i> </b><br /><i> Welcome to Shadowhunter Academy </i> was the first novella in Cassandra Clare's new bind up. I really enjoyed the take on the shadowhunter world from Simon's point of view. I can tell the new, and old, cast of characters are going to mold together perfectly. They all have such unique personalities that play off of each others really well. There were a couple of awkwardly worded scenes and dialogue that didn't flow, but other than that it was beautiful. I recommend starting this collection of novellas if you are a big geek, nerd, or Simon Lewis lover. <br /><i> I will write a full review on the bind up once I finish all of the novellas. </i></span>

<div id="review_1536190098" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1536190098" />
    <a title="Pinky" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27523984-pinky"><img alt="Pinky" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1489855494p2/27523984.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1536190098?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pinky" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pinky" href="/user/show/27523984-pinky">Pinky</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27523984-pinky?shelf=books-i-want-to-own">books-i-want-to-own</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1536190098" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4534043809778132623"> I don't know why, but recently, I have had a thing for nouvellas. Back in the day when I first started reading, I loved reading with physical books. I wasn't a huge fan of ebooks and reading online. And I still feel that way, but recently, I had no choice but to read on my phone because there are some short stories that haven't been released in a bind up. Or there are some really good books online that are not released in physical form. I really love The Mortal Instruments and The Infernal Devi</span>
  <span id="freeText4534043809778132623" style="display:none"> I don't know why, but recently, I have had a thing for nouvellas. Back in the day when I first started reading, I loved reading with physical books. I wasn't a huge fan of ebooks and reading online. And I still feel that way, but recently, I had no choice but to read on my phone because there are some short stories that haven't been released in a bind up. Or there are some really good books online that are not released in physical form. I really love The Mortal Instruments and The Infernal Devices. I knew that this series came out but I was waiting for the book bind-up. Michelle, one of my friends on Goodreads recommended this to me, but I was still waiting until the physical book with all of the nouvellas came out. But then I watched Christine's video, and she convinced me and I felt that I had to read this ASAP and catch up with everything because if you don't read this before Lady Midnight, apparently you will be spoiled... And I don't want that. (Christine is one of my favorite booktubers, her YouTube Channel is called Polandbananasbooks, if you haven't heard of her, I definitely recommend you watch her because she is awesome!)<br><br><b>I think I might jump into spoilers now because I NEED TO DISCUSS THIS BOOK!<br><br><i><b>“I am here to determine my relationship."</b></i></b><br><br> This is a story that takes place after a bunch of events from City of Heavenly Fire. Simon is the main character in this series. After losing his memory, he has to go to Shadowhunter Academy and learn to find himself along with learning how to fight demons and other things. He needs to find the inner hero that he once was and has to live through the pained looks of his loved ones. This is basically a book where we might get some insight on what happens to Simon and where will this series take us next.<br><br><i>
  <b>“Simon," Isabelle interrupted, "you're talking like a nerd."</b>
</i><br><br> The characters were all amazing, I loved everyone... OBVIOUSLY! Simon was awesome as always but I hated the fact that I had to see him suffer. The pain of not knowing anything and forgetting the most important things that have happened to you. The pain of forgetting the people you love is just so horrid. And seeing the others try to move past what happened hurts so much. Isabelle misses Simon and has to deal with the fact that he forgot about her... About them. We get to see a little bit of Jace, Clary, Alec and Isabelle and I loved that scene. <br><br>Reunited with Simon (Me in my dreams):<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455508575ra/18110369.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>“Hey, Clary. You take care of yourself," he said. "I know you can." He paused. "And take care of Jace, that poor, helpless blond."</b>
</i><br><br> I loved the part where Isabelle decides to walk into the classroom and tells everyone to back off from Simon. She is so awesome, beautiful, and fierce, I look up to her in ways because of this. Simon and Isabelle's lines to each other were painful. He wants to be the guy he used to be but he doesn't remember anything and he doesn't feel like he will be the hero. <br><br>Isabelle:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455508575ra/18110370.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>“None of this is fair. It isn't fair that part of your life was ripped from you. It's not fair that you were ripped away from me. I'm so angry Simon.” </b>
</i><br><br> I was glad that I listened to everyone and read this because I was missing out on so much. If you haven't read this short story or whatever it is called, I highly recommend you do so. It's best if you finish this series before Lady Midnight because of the spoilers. Also, you get to revisit the world and reunite with the characters you love! <br><br><i>
  <b>“Maybe warlocks only liked other warlocks. Though Magnus did seem to like Alec quite a lot.”</b>
</i><br><br><i>
  <b> P.S Happy Valentines Day! </b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455508576ra/18110371.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </span>
  <a data-text-id="4534043809778132623" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer479761079289232023">I loved this story! I specially adored seeing everyone again. <b>I missed them so, so much!</b> I also really enjoyed seeing the Academy and how it works <s>or how it tries to work</s>. <br/><br/>Catarina has confusing me at first but then she became the warlock I remembered! <b>George</b> surprised me, I ended up really liking him, I can see him and Simon being very good friends.   <span id="freeText479761079289232023" style="display:none">I loved this story! I specially adored seeing everyone again. <b>I missed them so, so much!</b> I also really enjoyed seeing the Academy and how it works <s>or how it tries to work</s>. <br /><br />Catarina has confusing me at first but then she became the warlock I remembered! <b>George</b> surprised me, I ended up really liking him, I can see him and Simon being very good friends. I really loved the way he spoke him mind about the way he saw things. But the way he's dealing with <b>Izzy</b>? I think he should tell to start again. If only she could forget the boy he once was and just enjoy meeting this new Simon it would me a lot easier. And speaking of Izzy, I loved her <i>class</i>! <br /><br /><b>
  <i>Sizzy for life</i>
</b><br /><br />PS. Does anyone remember why Alec has a problem with Simon? I'd like to know.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2565468854" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5016060370794801021"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He waved good-bye to all these people he barely knew and somehow loved anyway, and he hoped they could not tell how relieved he was to be going.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>Yikes, we aren’t off to a good start. Okay, this anthology picks up right after the events of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2544728646' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Heavenly Fire</a>, but Simon still doesn’t remember everything that happened, but he is now enrolled at the New York Institute. We get to meet so many new students, since the Shadowhunter world is in desperate need to replenish their fighters! </span>
  <span id="freeText5016060370794801021" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He waved good-bye to all these people he barely knew and somehow loved anyway, and he hoped they could not tell how relieved he was to be going.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />Yikes, we aren’t off to a good start. Okay, this anthology picks up right after the events of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2544728646" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Heavenly Fire</a>, but Simon still doesn’t remember everything that happened, but he is now enrolled at the New York Institute. We get to meet so many new students, since the Shadowhunter world is in desperate need to replenish their fighters! I already love George. I already hate Jon. I will say that at first, I was so happy with Izzy’s declaration of love for Simon, but the more and more I kept thinking about it, I kept realizing that I was showing double standards, because if a dude would have done that to a girl I would have really disliked it. I will say that I always appreciated that Simon is the *nerdy one* and Izzy is the *popular one* and how Cassie Clare really plays that opposite trope up to perfection, but Izzy’s speech was a little too much even for me. I want good angst, not forced angst. <br /><br /><a href="https://meltotheany.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/meltotheany/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.twitter.com/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://meltotheany.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UC4RbHEg_fH6CewJrh_0xJ9g" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a href="http://www.twitch.tv/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitch</a><br /><br />(I read this in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2564114842" rel="nofollow noopener">Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy</a>!) ✨</span>
  <a data-text-id="5016060370794801021" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Thibaut Nicodème" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22674620-thibaut-nicod-me"><img alt="Thibaut Nicodème" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1574079623p2/22674620.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1046301201?book_show_action=true">Sep 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Thibaut Nicodème" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Thibaut Nicodème" href="/user/show/22674620-thibaut-nicod-me">Thibaut Nicodème</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22674620-thibaut-nicod-me?shelf=snark">snark</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1046301201" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3742015648100884310">Full review <a href='http://snarktheater.tumblr.com/post/135067450731/tales-from-shadowhunter-academy-welcome-to' rel='nofollow noopener'>on my blog, the Snark Theater</a>.<br/><br/>So…this was on the verge of getting two-stars for being an unnecessary story about a character I don't like which undid said character's sacrifice and thus most of the consequences we had for <i>City of Heavenly Fire</i> at all. Because aside from the context, it starts out pretty okay. It's basically <i>Mean Girls</i> with Shadowhunters. And less witty.<br/><br/>But then the book kind of forgets that, in <i>Mean Girls</i>, the protagonist isn't in a school that will make her join the</span>
  <span id="freeText3742015648100884310" style="display:none">Full review <a href="http://snarktheater.tumblr.com/post/135067450731/tales-from-shadowhunter-academy-welcome-to" rel="nofollow noopener">on my blog, the Snark Theater</a>.<br /><br />So…this was on the verge of getting two-stars for being an unnecessary story about a character I don't like which undid said character's sacrifice and thus most of the consequences we had for <i>City of Heavenly Fire</i> at all. Because aside from the context, it starts out pretty okay. It's basically <i>Mean Girls</i> with Shadowhunters. And less witty.<br /><br />But then the book kind of forgets that, in <i>Mean Girls</i>, the protagonist isn't in a school that will make her join the Plastics when she graduates. Which is exactly what everything is wrong with Julie and Jon: their bigotry is entirely a byproduct of being Shadowhunters, and Simon and his new no-homo best buddy George are going to become Shadowhunters. You're not making a good case for the "Shadowhunters are morally complex" when they're also framed as the be-all, end-all, is what I'm getting at.<br /><br />Add the random Isabelle appearance at the end for a Sizzy break-up (which I'm sure won't last very long), completely wrecking the otherwise okay pacing of the story, and the need for several mentions of Jace's uncanny hotness even though Jace isn't even on the same continent, and I'm not feeling very indulgent towards this short story, or the rest of this series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3742015648100884310" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1124592121" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9716687719196700641">Well this is definitely not TMI....<i>and it is most certainly not my <b>beloved</b> TID</i>, but it was still okay. I've never been a huge fan of Simon, so I didn't really find this first installment of the Shadowhunter Academy books to be epic or anything, but it did have its moments of humor. </span>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('UQQZFGD4w4f9khG7bMIhY9ootD7Wmt4iUd78iImh83VsbSSzm7Feyl119GlXkfwGVnxJeJEpTjV72AZvrxeuog==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

  }

  <span id="freeText15726853882895258990" style="display:none">Hello Goodreadsers. Here's my official bio:<br /><br />"Cassandra Clare was born overseas and spent her early years traveling around the world with her family and several trunks of fantasy books. Cassandra worked for several years as an entertainment journalist for the Hollywood Reporter before turning her attention to fiction. She is the author of City of Bones, the first book in the Mortal Instruments trilogy and a New York Times bestseller. Cassandra lives with her fiance and their two cats in Massachusetts."<br /><br />You can find me online at <br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.cassandraclare.com">www.cassandraclare.com</a><br /><br />I have a blog:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://cassandraclare.livejournal.com/">http://cassandraclare.livejournal.com/</a><br /><br />and a Facebook:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/Cassandraclare">http://www.facebook.com/Cassandraclare</a><br /><br />and a Twitter:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.twitter.com/cassieclare">www.twitter.com/cassieclare</a><br /><br />I'll be available here on Goodreads to answer questions for a Goodreads Author Discussion starting September 18 — <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/37113.Q_A_with_Cassandra_Clare">http://www.goodreads.com/group/show/3...</a><br /><br />Go sign up so you don't miss the conversation when it starts!</span>

"You were never that smooth, Simon."<br />"Oh," said Simon. "Oh, thank God. I know you've had a lot of boyfriends. I remember that was a faerie, and"--another flash of memory, this time most unwelcome--"a...Lord Montgomery? You dated a member of the nobility? How am I ever going to compete with that?"<br />Isabelle still looked fond, but it was diluted with a good deal of impatience. "You're Lord Montgomery, Simon!&rdquo;</span>
